# Command Proof Log

**Change:** `habitat-grit-proof-repair`
**Status:** implementation rows recorded for native samples, Habitat wrapper
tool selection, wrong-namespace rejection, per-rule selector projection,
raw-direct non-claim, explicit Grit baseline behavior, injected row proof,
apply target-export/dry-run proof, live applied-diff proof, cold selected
post-apply gate proof, and current old-mechanism parity closure. Downstream
proof rows remain open.

`HGPR-APPLY-LIVE-COLD-GATES-2026-06-15` and
`HGPR-APPLY-P2-SELECTED-CHECK-GATE-COLD-PROOF-2026-06-15` use durable
command/lifecycle facts in this packet record. Older historical `/tmp/habitat-*`
artifact references are preserved as their original row context and are not new
evidence for the cold-gate repair unless a row explicitly restates them.

Current restack note for HG row proof sections: row-owned native fixture and
parser inventory entries below preserve their original pre-restack branch
evidence when explicitly labeled historical/pre-restack. Current restacked
shared wrapper selector, per-rule selector, explicit baseline file, baseline
integrity, and injected-row proof for the already-restacked HG rows is recorded
by `HGPR-HABITAT-GRIT-TOOL-2026-06-15`,
`HGPR-PER-RULE-SELECTORS-2026-06-15`,
`HGPR-BASELINE-FILES-2026-06-15`,
`HGPR-BASELINE-INTEGRITY-2026-06-15`, and
`HGPR-INJECTED-GRIT-ROWS-2026-06-15`. Direct raw Grit acquisition remains
`HGPR-RAW-GRIT-UNCLAIMED-2026-06-15`, and row-specific blockers/non-claims
still govern clean closure.

Each command proof row must include:

| Field | Required content |
| --- | --- |
| Proof id | Stable id referenced by matrix/tasks |
| Proof class | native sample / current-tree wrapper / raw acquisition / injected violation / baseline / parity / Nx scheduling / dry-run / applied diff / rollback / stale-record scan |
| Branch and commit | branch plus commit or dirty-state marker at execution time |
| Command | exact argv as executed |
| CWD | working directory |
| Env delta | relevant env additions or proof that none were set |
| Exit code | numeric exit code or signal/interruption class |
| Raw output artifact | repo-local workstream artifact or bounded excerpt; do not cite ephemeral scratch paths for new proof rows |
| Parsed summary | counts, ids, statuses, cache state, or selected rule ids |
| Cache/fresh status | required for Nx and Grit cache-sensitive probes |
| Duration/timing source | measured duration or explicit not recorded |
| Proof result | satisfied / failed / interrupted / unclaimed |
| Non-claim | what the command does not prove |
| Skipped-gate rationale | required when a planned proof is not run |
